Cluster Identify

Attributes and commands for putting a device into Identification mode (e.\+g. flashing a light). Command Identify

Command description for Identify Command Trigger\+Effect

Command description for Trigger\+Effect

Cluster Groups

Attributes and commands for group configuration and manipulation. Command Add\+Group

Command description for Add\+Group Command View\+Group

Command description for View\+Group Command Get\+Group\+Membership

Command description for Get\+Group\+Membership Command Remove\+Group

Command description for Remove\+Group Command Remove\+All\+Groups

Command description for Remove\+All\+Groups Command Add\+Group\+If\+Identifying

Command description for Add\+Group\+If\+Identifying

Cluster Scenes

Attributes and commands for scene configuration and manipulation. Command Add\+Scene

Add a scene to the scene table. Extension field sets are supported, and are inputed as \textquotesingle{}\{\char`\"{}\+Cluster\+ID\char`\"{}\+: VALUE, \char`\"{}\+Attribute\+Value\+List\char`\"{}\+:\mbox{[}\{\char`\"{}\+Attribute\+Id\char`\"{}\+: VALUE, \char`\"{}\+Attribute\+Value\char`\"{}\+: VALUE\}\mbox{]}\}\textquotesingle{} Command View\+Scene

Retrieves the requested scene entry from its Scene table. Command Remove\+Scene

Removes the requested scene entry, corresponding to the value of the Group\+ID field, from its Scene Table Command Remove\+All\+Scenes

Remove all scenes, corresponding to the value of the Group\+ID field, from its Scene Table Command Store\+Scene

Adds the scene entry into its Scene Table along with all extension field sets corresponding to the current state of other clusters on the same endpoint Command Recall\+Scene

Set the attributes and corresponding state for each other cluster implemented on the endpoint accordingly to the resquested scene entry in the Scene Table Command Get\+Scene\+Membership

Get an unused scene identifier when no commissioning tool is in the network, or for a commissioning tool to get the used scene identifiers within a certain group Command Enhanced\+Add\+Scene

Allows a scene to be added using a finer scene transition time than the Add\+Scene command. Command Enhanced\+View\+Scene

Allows a scene to be retrieved using a finer scene transition time than the View\+Scene command Command Copy\+Scene

Allows a client to efficiently copy scenes from one group/scene identifier pair to another group/scene identifier pair.

Cluster On/\+Off

Attributes and commands for switching devices between \textquotesingle{}On\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}Off\textquotesingle{} states. Command Off

On receipt of this command, a device SHALL enter its ‘\+Off’ state. This state is device dependent, but it is recommended that it is used for power off or similar functions. On receipt of the Off command, the On\+Time attribute SHALL be set to 0. Command On

On receipt of this command, a device SHALL enter its ‘\+On’ state. This state is device dependent, but it is recommended that it is used for power on or similar functions. On receipt of the On command, if the value of the On\+Time attribute is equal to 0, the device SHALL set the Off\+Wait\+Time attribute to 0. Command Toggle

On receipt of this command, if a device is in its ‘\+Off’ state it SHALL enter its ‘\+On’ state. Otherwise, if it is in its ‘\+On’ state it SHALL enter its ‘\+Off’ state. On receipt of the Toggle command, if the value of the On\+Off attribute is equal to FALSE and if the value of the On\+Time attribute is equal to 0, the device SHALL set the Off\+Wait\+Time attribute to 0. If the value of the On\+Off attribute is equal to TRUE, the On\+Time attribute SHALL be set to 0. Command Off\+With\+Effect

The Off\+With\+Effect command allows devices to be turned off using enhanced ways of fading. Command On\+With\+Recall\+Global\+Scene

The On\+With\+Recall\+Global\+Scene command allows the recall of the settings when the device was turned off. Command On\+With\+Timed\+Off

The On\+With\+Timed\+Off command allows devices to be turned on for a specific duration with a guarded off duration so that SHOULD the device be subsequently switched off, further On\+With\+Timed\+Off commands, received during this time, are prevented from turning the devices back on.

Cluster On/off Switch Configuration

Attributes and commands for configuring On/\+Off switching devices.

Cluster Level Control

Attributes and commands for controlling devices that can be set to a level between fully \textquotesingle{}On\textquotesingle{} and fully \textquotesingle{}Off.\textquotesingle{} Command Move\+To\+Level

Command description for Move\+To\+Level Command Move

Command description for Move Command Step

Command description for Step Command Stop

Command description for Stop Command Move\+To\+Level\+With\+On\+Off

Command description for Move\+To\+Level\+With\+On\+Off Command Move\+With\+On\+Off

Command description for Move\+With\+On\+Off Command Step\+With\+On\+Off

Command description for Step\+With\+On\+Off Command Stop\+With\+On\+Off

Command description for Stop\+With\+On\+Off Command Move\+To\+Closest\+Frequency

Change the currrent frequency to the provided one, or a close approximation if the exact provided one is not possible.

Cluster Binary Input (Basic)

An interface for reading the value of a binary measurement and accessing various characteristics of that measurement.

Cluster Descriptor

The Descriptor Cluster is meant to replace the support from the Zigbee Device Object (ZDO) for describing a node, its endpoints and clusters.

Cluster Binding

The Binding Cluster is meant to replace the support from the Zigbee Device Object (ZDO) for supporting the binding table.

Cluster Access Control

The Access Control Cluster exposes a data model view of a Node\textquotesingle{}s Access Control List (ACL), which codifies the rules used to manage and enforce Access Control for the Node\textquotesingle{}s endpoints and their associated cluster instances.

Cluster Actions

This cluster provides a standardized way for a Node (typically a Bridge, but could be any Node) to expose action information. Command Instant\+Action

This command triggers an action (state change) on the involved endpoints. Command Instant\+Action\+With\+Transition

This command triggers an action (state change) on the involved endpoints, with a specified time to transition from the current state to the new state. Command Start\+Action

This command triggers the commencement of an action on the involved endpoints. Command Start\+Action\+With\+Duration

This command triggers the commencement of an action (with a duration) on the involved endpoints. Command Stop\+Action

This command stops the ongoing action on the involved endpoints. Command Pause\+Action

This command pauses an ongoing action. Command Pause\+Action\+With\+Duration

This command pauses an ongoing action with a duration. Command Resume\+Action

This command resumes a previously paused action. Command Enable\+Action

This command enables a certain action or automation. Command Enable\+Action\+With\+Duration

This command enables a certain action or automation with a duration. Command Disable\+Action

This command disables a certain action or automation. Command Disable\+Action\+With\+Duration

This command disables a certain action or automation with a duration.

Cluster Basic Information

This cluster provides attributes and events for determining basic information about Nodes, which supports both Commissioning and operational determination of Node characteristics, such as Vendor ID, Product ID and serial number, which apply to the whole Node. Also allows setting user device information such as location.

Cluster OTA Software Update Provider

Provides an interface for providing OTA software updates Command Query\+Image

Determine availability of a new Software Image Command Apply\+Update\+Request

Determine next action to take for a downloaded Software Image Command Notify\+Update\+Applied

Notify OTA Provider that an update was applied

Cluster OTA Software Update Requestor

Provides an interface for downloading and applying OTA software updates Command Announce\+OTAProvider

Announce the presence of an OTA Provider

Cluster Localization Configuration

Nodes should be expected to be deployed to any and all regions of the world. These global regions may have differing common languages, units of measurements, and numerical formatting standards. As such, Nodes that visually or audibly convey information need a mechanism by which they can be configured to use a user’s preferred language, units, etc

Cluster Time Format Localization

Nodes should be expected to be deployed to any and all regions of the world. These global regions may have differing preferences for how dates and times are conveyed. As such, Nodes that visually or audibly convey time information need a mechanism by which they can be configured to use a user’s preferred format.

Cluster Unit Localization

Nodes should be expected to be deployed to any and all regions of the world. These global regions may have differing preferences for the units in which values are conveyed in communication to a user. As such, Nodes that visually or audibly convey measurable values to the user need a mechanism by which they can be configured to use a user’s preferred unit.

Cluster Power Source Configuration

This cluster is used to describe the configuration and capabilities of a Device\textquotesingle{}s power system.

Cluster Power Source

This cluster is used to describe the configuration and capabilities of a physical power source that provides power to the Node.

Cluster General Commissioning

This cluster is used to manage global aspects of the Commissioning flow. Command Arm\+Fail\+Safe

Arm the persistent fail-\/safe timer with an expiry time of now + Expiry\+Length\+Seconds using device clock Command Set\+Regulatory\+Config

Set the regulatory configuration to be used during commissioning Command Commissioning\+Complete

Signals the Server that the Client has successfully completed all steps of Commissioning/\+Recofiguration needed during fail-\/safe period.

Cluster Network Commissioning

Functionality to configure, enable, disable network credentials and access on a Matter device. Command Scan\+Networks

Detemine the set of networks the device sees as available. Command Add\+Or\+Update\+Wi\+Fi\+Network

Add or update the credentials for a given Wi-\/\+Fi network. Command Add\+Or\+Update\+Thread\+Network

Add or update the credentials for a given Thread network. Command Remove\+Network

Remove the definition of a given network (including its credentials). Command Connect\+Network

Connect to the specified network, using previously-\/defined credentials. Command Reorder\+Network

Modify the order in which networks will be presented in the Networks attribute.

Cluster Diagnostic Logs

The cluster provides commands for retrieving unstructured diagnostic logs from a Node that may be used to aid in diagnostics. Command Retrieve\+Logs\+Request

Retrieving diagnostic logs from a Node

Cluster General Diagnostics

The General Diagnostics Cluster, along with other diagnostics clusters, provide a means to acquire standardized diagnostics metrics that MAY be used by a Node to assist a user or Administrative Node in diagnosing potential problems. Command Test\+Event\+Trigger

Provide a means for certification tests to trigger some test-\/plan-\/specific events

Cluster Software Diagnostics

The Software Diagnostics Cluster provides a means to acquire standardized diagnostics metrics that MAY be used by a Node to assist a user or Administrative Node in diagnosing potential problems. Command Reset\+Watermarks

Reception of this command SHALL reset the values\+: The Stack\+Free\+Minimum field of the Thread\+Metrics attribute, Current\+Heap\+High\+Water\+Mark attribute.

Cluster Thread Network Diagnostics

The Thread Network Diagnostics Cluster provides a means to acquire standardized diagnostics metrics that MAY be used by a Node to assist a user or Administrative Node in diagnosing potential problems Command Reset\+Counts

Reception of this command SHALL reset the Overrun\+Count attributes to 0

Cluster Wi\+Fi Network Diagnostics

The Wi-\/\+Fi Network Diagnostics Cluster provides a means to acquire standardized diagnostics metrics that MAY be used by a Node to assist a user or Administrative Node in diagnosing potential problems. Command Reset\+Counts

Reception of this command SHALL reset the Breacon and Packet related count attributes to 0

Cluster Ethernet Network Diagnostics

The Ethernet Network Diagnostics Cluster provides a means to acquire standardized diagnostics metrics that MAY be used by a Node to assist a user or Administrative Node in diagnosing potential problems. Command Reset\+Counts

Reception of this command SHALL reset the attributes\+: Packet\+Rx\+Count, Packet\+Tx\+Count, Tx\+Err\+Count, Collision\+Count, Overrun\+Count to 0

Cluster Bridged Device Basic Information

This Cluster serves two purposes towards a Node communicating with a Bridge\+: indicate that the functionality on the Endpoint where it is placed (and its Parts) is bridged from a non-\/\+CHIP technology; and provide a centralized collection of attributes that the Node MAY collect to aid in conveying information regarding the Bridged Device to a user, such as the vendor name, the model name, or user-\/assigned name.

Cluster Switch

This cluster exposes interactions with a switch device, for the purpose of using those interactions by other devices. Two types of switch devices are supported\+: latching switch (e.\+g. rocker switch) and momentary switch (e.\+g. push button), distinguished with their feature flags. Interactions with the switch device are exposed as attributes (for the latching switch) and as events (for both types of switches). An interested party MAY subscribe to these attributes/events and thus be informed of the interactions, and can perform actions based on this, for example by sending commands to perform an action such as controlling a light or a window shade.

Cluster Administrator Commissioning

Commands to trigger a Node to allow a new Administrator to commission it. Command Open\+Commissioning\+Window

This command is used by a current Administrator to instruct a Node to go into commissioning mode using enhanced commissioning method. Command Open\+Basic\+Commissioning\+Window

This command is used by a current Administrator to instruct a Node to go into commissioning mode using basic commissioning method, if the node supports it. Command Revoke\+Commissioning

This command is used by a current Administrator to instruct a Node to revoke any active Open Commissioning Window or Open Basic Commissioning Window command.

Cluster Operational Credentials

This cluster is used to add or remove Operational Credentials on a Commissionee or Node, as well as manage the associated Fabrics. Command Attestation\+Request

Sender is requesting attestation information from the receiver. Command Certificate\+Chain\+Request

Sender is requesting a device attestation certificate from the receiver. Command CSRRequest

Sender is requesting a certificate signing request (CSR) from the receiver. Command Add\+NOC

Sender is requesting to add the new node operational certificates. Command Update\+NOC

Sender is requesting to update the node operational certificates. Command Update\+Fabric\+Label

This command SHALL be used by an Administrative Node to set the user-\/visible Label field for a given Fabric, as reflected by entries in the Fabrics attribute. Command Remove\+Fabric

This command is used by Administrative Nodes to remove a given fabric index and delete all associated fabric-\/scoped data. Command Add\+Trusted\+Root\+Certificate

This command SHALL add a Trusted Root CA Certificate, provided as its CHIP Certificate representation.

Cluster Group Key Management

The Group Key Management Cluster is the mechanism by which group keys are managed. Command Key\+Set\+Write

Write a new set of keys for the given key set id. Command Key\+Set\+Read

Read the keys for a given key set id. Command Key\+Set\+Remove

Revoke a Root Key from a Group Command Key\+Set\+Read\+All\+Indices

Return the list of Group Key Sets associated with the accessing fabric

Cluster Fixed Label

The Fixed Label Cluster provides a feature for the device to tag an endpoint with zero or more read only labels.

Cluster User Label

The User Label Cluster provides a feature to tag an endpoint with zero or more labels.

Cluster Boolean State

This cluster provides an interface to a boolean state called State\+Value.

Cluster Mode Select

Attributes and commands for selecting a mode from a list of supported options. Command Change\+To\+Mode

On receipt of this command, if the New\+Mode field matches the Mode field in an entry of the Supported\+Modes list, the server SHALL set the Current\+Mode attribute to the New\+Mode value, otherwise, the server SHALL respond with an INVALID\+\_\+\+COMMAND status response.

Cluster Door Lock

An interface to a generic way to secure a door Command Lock\+Door

This command causes the lock device to lock the door. Command Unlock\+Door

This command causes the lock device to unlock the door. Command Unlock\+With\+Timeout

This command causes the lock device to unlock the door with a timeout parameter. Command Set\+Week\+Day\+Schedule

Set a weekly repeating schedule for a specified user. Command Get\+Week\+Day\+Schedule

Retrieve the specific weekly schedule for the specific user. Command Clear\+Week\+Day\+Schedule

Clear the specific weekly schedule or all weekly schedules for the specific user. Command Set\+Year\+Day\+Schedule

Set a time-\/specific schedule ID for a specified user. Command Get\+Year\+Day\+Schedule

Returns the year day schedule data for the specified schedule and user indexes. Command Clear\+Year\+Day\+Schedule

Clears the specific year day schedule or all year day schedules for the specific user. Command Set\+Holiday\+Schedule

Set the holiday Schedule by specifying local start time and local end time with respect to any Lock Operating Mode. Command Get\+Holiday\+Schedule

Get the holiday schedule for the specified index. Command Clear\+Holiday\+Schedule

Clears the holiday schedule or all holiday schedules. Command Set\+User

Set User into the lock. Command Get\+User

Retrieve User. Command Clear\+User

Clears a User or all Users. Command Set\+Credential

Set a credential (e.\+g. PIN, RFID, Fingerprint, etc.) into the lock for a new user, existing user, or Programming\+User. Command Get\+Credential\+Status

Retrieve the status of a particular credential (e.\+g. PIN, RFID, Fingerprint, etc.) by index. Command Clear\+Credential

Clear one, one type, or all credentials except Programming\+PIN credential.

Cluster Window Covering

Provides an interface for controlling and adjusting automatic window coverings. Command Up\+Or\+Open

Moves window covering to Installed\+Open\+Limit\+Lift and Installed\+Open\+Limit\+Tilt Command Down\+Or\+Close

Moves window covering to Installed\+Closed\+Limit\+Lift and Installed\+Close\+Limit\+Tilt Command Stop\+Motion

Stop any adjusting of window covering Command Go\+To\+Lift\+Value

Go to lift value specified Command Go\+To\+Lift\+Percentage

Go to lift percentage specified Command Go\+To\+Tilt\+Value

Go to tilt value specified Command Go\+To\+Tilt\+Percentage

Go to tilt percentage specified

Cluster Barrier Control

This cluster provides control of a barrier (garage door). Command Barrier\+Control\+Go\+To\+Percent

Command to instruct a barrier to go to a percent open state. Command Barrier\+Control\+Stop

Command that instructs the barrier to stop moving.

Cluster Pump Configuration and Control

An interface for configuring and controlling pumps.

Cluster Thermostat

An interface for configuring and controlling the functionality of a thermostat. Command Setpoint\+Raise\+Lower

Command description for Setpoint\+Raise\+Lower Command Set\+Weekly\+Schedule

Command description for Set\+Weekly\+Schedule Command Get\+Weekly\+Schedule

Command description for Get\+Weekly\+Schedule Command Clear\+Weekly\+Schedule

The Clear Weekly Schedule command is used to clear the weekly schedule.

Cluster Fan Control

An interface for controlling a fan in a heating/cooling system.

Cluster Thermostat User Interface Configuration

An interface for configuring the user interface of a thermostat (which may be remote from the thermostat).

Cluster Color Control

Attributes and commands for controlling the color properties of a color-\/capable light. Command Move\+To\+Hue

Move to specified hue. Command Move\+Hue

Move hue up or down at specified rate. Command Step\+Hue

Step hue up or down by specified size at specified rate. Command Move\+To\+Saturation

Move to specified saturation. Command Move\+Saturation

Move saturation up or down at specified rate. Command Step\+Saturation

Step saturation up or down by specified size at specified rate. Command Move\+To\+Hue\+And\+Saturation

Move to hue and saturation. Command Move\+To\+Color

Move to specified color. Command Move\+Color

Moves the color. Command Step\+Color

Steps the lighting to a specific color. Command Move\+To\+Color\+Temperature

Move to a specific color temperature. Command Enhanced\+Move\+To\+Hue

Command description for Enhanced\+Move\+To\+Hue Command Enhanced\+Move\+Hue

Command description for Enhanced\+Move\+Hue Command Enhanced\+Step\+Hue

Command description for Enhanced\+Step\+Hue Command Enhanced\+Move\+To\+Hue\+And\+Saturation

Command description for Enhanced\+Move\+To\+Hue\+And\+Saturation Command Color\+Loop\+Set

Command description for Color\+Loop\+Set Command Stop\+Move\+Step

Command description for Stop\+Move\+Step Command Move\+Color\+Temperature

Command description for Move\+Color\+Temperature Command Step\+Color\+Temperature

Command description for Step\+Color\+Temperature

Cluster Ballast Configuration

Attributes and commands for configuring a lighting ballast.

Cluster Illuminance Measurement

Attributes and commands for configuring the measurement of illuminance, and reporting illuminance measurements.

Cluster Temperature Measurement

Attributes and commands for configuring the measurement of temperature, and reporting temperature measurements.

Cluster Pressure Measurement

Attributes and commands for configuring the measurement of pressure, and reporting pressure measurements.

Cluster Flow Measurement

Attributes and commands for configuring the measurement of flow, and reporting flow measurements.

Cluster Relative Humidity Measurement

Attributes and commands for configuring the measurement of relative humidity, and reporting relative humidity measurements.

Cluster Occupancy Sensing

Attributes and commands for configuring occupancy sensing, and reporting occupancy status.

Cluster Wake on LAN

This cluster provides an interface for managing low power mode on a device that supports the Wake On LAN protocol.

Cluster Channel

This cluster provides an interface for controlling the current Channel on a device. Command Change\+Channel

Change the channel on the media player to the channel case-\/insensitive exact matching the value passed as an argument. Command Change\+Channel\+By\+Number

Change the channel on the media plaeyer to the channel with the given Number in the Channel\+List attribute. Command Skip\+Channel

This command provides channel up and channel down functionality, but allows channel index jumps of size Count. When the value of the increase or decrease is larger than the number of channels remaining in the given direction, then the behavior SHALL be to return to the beginning (or end) of the channel list and continue. For example, if the current channel is at index 0 and count value of -\/1 is given, then the current channel should change to the last channel.

Cluster Target Navigator

This cluster provides an interface for UX navigation within a set of targets on a device or endpoint. Command Navigate\+Target

Upon receipt, this SHALL navigation the UX to the target identified.

Cluster Media Playback

This cluster provides an interface for controlling Media Playback (PLAY, PAUSE, etc) on a media device such as a TV or Speaker. Command Play

Upon receipt, this SHALL play media. Command Pause

Upon receipt, this SHALL pause media. Command Stop

Upon receipt, this SHALL stop media. User experience is context-\/specific. This will often navigate the user back to the location where media was originally launched. Command Start\+Over

Upon receipt, this SHALL Start Over with the current media playback item. Command Previous

Upon receipt, this SHALL cause the handler to be invoked for \char`\"{}\+Previous\char`\"{}. User experience is context-\/specific. This will often Go back to the previous media playback item. Command Next

Upon receipt, this SHALL cause the handler to be invoked for \char`\"{}\+Next\char`\"{}. User experience is context-\/specific. This will often Go forward to the next media playback item. Command Rewind

Upon receipt, this SHALL Rewind through media. Different Rewind speeds can be used on the TV based upon the number of sequential calls to this function. This is to avoid needing to define every speed now (multiple fast, slow motion, etc). Command Fast\+Forward

Upon receipt, this SHALL Advance through media. Different FF speeds can be used on the TV based upon the number of sequential calls to this function. This is to avoid needing to define every speed now (multiple fast, slow motion, etc). Command Skip\+Forward

Upon receipt, this SHALL Skip forward in the media by the given number of seconds, using the data as follows\+: Command Skip\+Backward

Upon receipt, this SHALL Skip backward in the media by the given number of seconds, using the data as follows\+: Command Seek

Upon receipt, this SHALL Skip backward in the media by the given number of seconds, using the data as follows\+:

Cluster Media Input

This cluster provides an interface for controlling the Input Selector on a media device such as a TV. Command Select\+Input

Upon receipt, this SHALL change the input on the media device to the input at a specific index in the Input List. Command Show\+Input\+Status

Upon receipt, this SHALL display the active status of the input list on screen. Command Hide\+Input\+Status

Upon receipt, this SHALL hide the input list from the screen. Command Rename\+Input

Upon receipt, this SHALL rename the input at a specific index in the Input List. Updates to the input name SHALL appear in the TV settings menus.

Cluster Low Power

This cluster provides an interface for managing low power mode on a device. Command Sleep

This command shall put the device into low power mode.

Cluster Keypad Input

This cluster provides an interface for controlling a device like a TV using action commands such as UP, DOWN, and SELECT. Command Send\+Key

Upon receipt, this SHALL process a keycode as input to the media device.

Cluster Content Launcher

This cluster provides an interface for launching content on a media player device such as a TV or Speaker. Command Launch\+Content

Upon receipt, this SHALL launch the specified content with optional search criteria. Command Launch\+URL

Upon receipt, this SHALL launch content from the specified URL.

Cluster Audio Output

This cluster provides an interface for controlling the Output on a media device such as a TV. Command Select\+Output

Upon receipt, this SHALL change the output on the media device to the output at a specific index in the Output List. Command Rename\+Output

Upon receipt, this SHALL rename the output at a specific index in the Output List. Updates to the output name SHALL appear in the TV settings menus.

Cluster Application Launcher

This cluster provides an interface for launching content on a media player device such as a TV or Speaker. Command Launch\+App

Upon receipt, this SHALL launch the specified app with optional data. The TV Device SHALL launch and bring to foreground the identified application in the command if the application is not already launched and in foreground. The TV Device SHALL update state attribute on the Application Basic cluster of the Endpoint corresponding to the launched application. This command returns a Launch Response. Command Stop\+App

Upon receipt on a Video Player endpoint this SHALL stop the specified application if it is running. Command Hide\+App

Upon receipt on a Video Player endpoint this SHALL hide the specified application if it is running and visible.

Cluster Application Basic

This cluster provides information about an application running on a TV or media player device which is represented as an endpoint.

Cluster Account Login

This cluster provides commands that facilitate user account login on a Content App or a node. For example, a Content App running on a Video Player device, which is represented as an endpoint (see \mbox{[}TV Architecture\mbox{]}), can use this cluster to help make the user account on the Content App match the user account on the Client. Command Get\+Setup\+PIN

Upon receipt, the Content App checks if the account associated with the client Temp Account Identifier Rotating ID is the same acount that is active on the given Content App. If the accounts are the same, then the Content App includes the Setup PIN in the Get\+Setup\+PIN Response. Command Login

Upon receipt, the Content App checks if the account associated with the client’s Temp Account Identifier (Rotating ID) has a current active Setup PIN with the given value. If the Setup PIN is valid for the user account associated with the Temp Account Identifier, then the Content App MAY make that user account active. Command Logout

The purpose of this command is to instruct the Content App to clear the current user account. This command SHOULD be used by clients of a Content App to indicate the end of a user session.

Cluster Electrical Measurement

Attributes related to the electrical properties of a device. This cluster is used by power outlets and other devices that need to provide instantaneous data as opposed to metrology data which should be retrieved from the metering cluster.. Command Get\+Profile\+Info\+Command

A function which retrieves the power profiling information from the electrical measurement server. Command Get\+Measurement\+Profile\+Command

A function which retrieves an electricity measurement profile from the electricity measurement server for a specific attribute Id requested.

Cluster Unit Testing

The Test Cluster is meant to validate the generated code Command Test

Simple command without any parameters and without a specific response Command Test\+Not\+Handled

Simple command without any parameters and without a specific response not handled by the server Command Test\+Specific

Simple command without any parameters and with a specific response Command Test\+Unknown\+Command

Simple command that should not be added to the server. Command Test\+Add\+Arguments

Command that takes two arguments and returns their sum. Command Test\+Simple\+Argument\+Request

Command that takes an argument which is bool Command Test\+Struct\+Array\+Argument\+Request

Command that takes various arguments that are arrays, including an array of structs which have a list member. Command Test\+Struct\+Argument\+Request

Command that takes an argument which is struct. The response echoes the \textquotesingle{}b\textquotesingle{} field of the single arg. Command Test\+Nested\+Struct\+Argument\+Request

Command that takes an argument which is nested struct. The response echoes the \textquotesingle{}b\textquotesingle{} field of ar1.\+c. Command Test\+List\+Struct\+Argument\+Request

Command that takes an argument which is a list of structs. The response returns false if there is some struct in the list whose \textquotesingle{}b\textquotesingle{} field is false, and true otherwise (including if the list is empty). Command Test\+List\+Int8\+UArgument\+Request

Command that takes an argument which is a list of INT8U. The response returns false if the list contains a 0 in it, true otherwise (including if the list is empty). Command Test\+Nested\+Struct\+List\+Argument\+Request

Command that takes an argument which is a Nested Struct List. The response returns false if there is some struct in arg1 (either directly in arg1.\+c or in the arg1.\+d list) whose \textquotesingle{}b\textquotesingle{} field is false, and true otherwise. Command Test\+List\+Nested\+Struct\+List\+Argument\+Request

Command that takes an argument which is a list of Nested Struct List. The response returns false if there is some struct in arg1 (either directly in as the \textquotesingle{}c\textquotesingle{} field of an entry \textquotesingle{}d\textquotesingle{} list of an entry) whose \textquotesingle{}b\textquotesingle{} field is false, and true otherwise (including if the list is empty). Command Test\+List\+Int8\+UReverse\+Request

Command that takes an argument which is a list of INT8U and expects a response that reverses the list. Command Test\+Enums\+Request

Command that sends a vendor id and an enum. The server is expected to echo them back. Command Test\+Nullable\+Optional\+Request

Command that takes an argument which is nullable and optional. The response returns a boolean indicating whether the argument was present, if that\textquotesingle{}s true a boolean indicating whether the argument was null, and if that\textquotesingle{} false the argument it received. Command Test\+Complex\+Nullable\+Optional\+Request

Command that takes various arguments which can be nullable and/or optional. The response returns information about which things were received and what their state was. Command Simple\+Struct\+Echo\+Request

Command that takes an argument which is a struct. The response echoes the struct back. Command Timed\+Invoke\+Request

Command that just responds with a success status if the timed invoke conditions are met. Command Test\+Simple\+Optional\+Argument\+Request

Command that takes an optional argument which is bool. It responds with a success value if the optional is set to any value. Command Test\+Emit\+Test\+Event\+Request

Command that takes identical arguments to the fields of the Test\+Event and logs the Test\+Event to the buffer. Command returns an event ID as the response. Command Test\+Emit\+Test\+Fabric\+Scoped\+Event\+Request

Command that takes identical arguments to the fields of the Test\+Fabric\+Scoped\+Event and logs the Test\+Fabric\+Scoped\+Event to the buffer. Command returns an event ID as the response.

Represents the Matter-\/specific components of an X.\+509 Distinguished Name.

Cluster Groups Attributes and commands for group configuration and manipulation.

Cluster Diagnostic Logs The cluster provides commands for retrieving unstructured diagnostic logs from a Node that may be used to aid in diagnostics.

Cluster General Diagnostics The General Diagnostics Cluster, along with other diagnostics clusters, provide a means to acquire standardized diagnostics metrics that MAY be used by a Node to assist a user or Administrative Node in diagnosing potential problems.

Cluster Software Diagnostics The Software Diagnostics Cluster provides a means to acquire standardized diagnostics metrics that MAY be used by a Node to assist a user or Administrative Node in diagnosing potential problems.

Cluster Thread Network Diagnostics The Thread Network Diagnostics Cluster provides a means to acquire standardized diagnostics metrics that MAY be used by a Node to assist a user or Administrative Node in diagnosing potential problems

Cluster Ethernet Network Diagnostics The Ethernet Network Diagnostics Cluster provides a means to acquire standardized diagnostics metrics that MAY be used by a Node to assist a user or Administrative Node in diagnosing potential problems.

Cluster Administrator Commissioning Commands to trigger a Node to allow a new Administrator to commission it.

Cluster Operational Credentials This cluster is used to add or remove Operational Credentials on a Commissionee or Node, as well as manage the associated Fabrics.

Cluster Group Key Management The Group Key Management Cluster is the mechanism by which group keys are managed.

Cluster Mode Select Attributes and commands for selecting a mode from a list of supported options.
